Adano65_1RecordedfromVisitQ2RRNW6 - 4 You see the whole thing is each one of us is like a little spark and then as the spark gets bigger by exposure to other sparks before you know it, it becomes a flame. Now eight or ten years ago I don’t think anyone was ready for these men, they wouldn’t comprehend what they were going to teach, but then again you need sort of a movement prior to their presence or prior to their coming to sort of lay the groundwork, lay sort of a challenge in ourselves. So we had what we call a beatnik movement, we had the hippie movement, and now we have what is called gelling of this consciousness. We find all of the students in the universities are all reaching out to really explore themselves for the first time. As long as you have these men living and demonstrating this capacity, you find being exposed to that prior movement, you have something now to compare, before you had nothing to compare, you see? 10 Story of the monk who had to quit and met Adano. They meditated on the reservations. He had three comparisons: walking up and down due to his original training, exposure to people on the reservation who resort to peyote (psychedelic), he saw the devotion / simplicity and the disadvantage which was the extrasensory awareness would not stay after the “meetings.” 13 Symbology of Peter crucified upside down. Jesus is the symbolism of pure intuition, direct perception from within oneself, free from repercussion of thinking. Peter was a demonstration of dogged will. It is upon concentrated will that intuitive consciousness has an opportunity to regulate life. 15 Will is a combination of desire plus energy because your are a living model of consciousness and congealed energy in the form of matter. The trick of it, what we call Maya or the relativity of it is how to recognize it. The only way to recognize this is when you can stop the feeling. If you have the power to regulate your will, you control feeling. We want to develop will first, so the true feeling can come out. Peter preferred to be crucified upside down because Will contains some Ego in it, it is never free because it requires a desire pattern to drive it. Until we surrender this Will and accept Divine Will, “not my will but the Cosmic Will be done.” 20 As long as there is ego in the will, intuition cannot control our life. Drugs create a suspension, a helpless being, semi-paralysis of the organs. If you surrender to Cosmic Will, then you are relaxing and things are falling into place, you feel upside down. Then you have performed symbolically the upside down crucifixion of Peter. We can’t be free until this occurs, but we need Will to enforce a certain level of understanding, but then we need to tear it down to get to the next level of understanding. You never really crash. What really feels like crashing is inwardly we feel the futility of struggle. Not to know what you are doing or why you are doing it builds up such a tremendous anxiety in us that automatically we are starting to collapse. That is the core of fear. There is no reason to fear, but it is the unknown quantity X that keeps us agitated. Why are we not getting results? Why can’t we eat the seed right away? Why do I have to plant it? 25 We are trying to “stick out” the value of human life as a human being. We have to work with the consciousness even under the hustle and bustle of everyday existence. You are proving the other half of your nature, the universe was made for man, not man for the universe. The Saints know that and go back to live with people. 30 People are grasping for offspring to have something better than them. If we were living in the etheric body, we wouldn’t choose this planet with all these problems and sickness. The Masters are masters of life engineering, the art of behavior. Origins of all religions. All Masters teach one basic truth that is exposed by the human form and by the human form it is adulterated. Jesus demonstrated Masterhood to a particular group of people in a particular culture at a particular time. The 12 disciples didn’t even get realization until he left the body, only one got it when he was in the body (the thief on the cross). We don’t know how to swim the river of life through conscious feeling and conscious will, therefore we are stuck in the mud of resistance. Yet if we can swim through it, we are free. The only real place you are going is HERE and the only real feeling is NOW. The only true action is Joy of Awareness, being alive. If you are aware of your existence, you want Joy. You can feel and taste texture, it is pulsating. Then you know you are truly experiencing, “I have come that you may have life more abundantly.” 40 Self awareness is opening up in your for you to experience the reality of life vibration around you full for the first time. Alive to the point of bursting. Joy is aliveness. Joy is now and here. Whatever you are doing, you are doing it with the fullness of Joy. You are building a bank account of Joy. It is more the understanding of happiness than the pursuit of happiness. Happiness IS. Happiness exists as a feeling in the contents of mind. You use mind to perceive. When you perceive you retain the perceptions in the reservoir of mind. You get the happiness from this reservoir. Seeing existence as a movie. All these things come to pass, but not to stay. 45 Questions and answers: Sita. Ram Ram Sita Ram. Ram or Rama was the personification of God in Man as the ideal husband. Sita was the personification of God in woman as the ideal wife. Adano tells the entire story of the Ramayana in modern terms including explaining Hanuman, the Monkey god.

There are many more scales than seven, there are unlimited scales. Meditation helps you to prepare yourself to bring it in. You are all brothers and sisters of Light, Pure Energy. In Devotion there is no resistance, it’s like water, it just flows. He wasn’t talking about this. 1:23 The moment a man of truth, or anyone who is interested in the truth of his existence, the moment he gets together in the Consciousness of I, the consciousness of his own self, and to listen to his own name, that’s the vibration, in My Name, that is Cosmic Vibration, that’s the vibration or frequency of the I-ness in you. Adano65_06_02ManisSoulQ1RRNW6 - Question: Why is it I can’t get past a certain state of development? Why can’t I get the experience to back it up? I am going to give the reason why the student cannot get past the intellectual stage into the spiritual experience because there is a basic law there. That law is sometimes called Satan, Devil, or the Divine Examiner. But it is called by the metaphysician or cosmic science, the Principle of Ramm. This particular part is called the Primary Principle, like the primary function in a coil because it involves a particular force in the mechanism. And the second part is SLR. This is called the Secondary. R stands for Resistance. The basic intrinsic resistance in all structure by the very art of creation exists as is. God cannot destroy His devils because He is devil manifest also. You see? He cannot come into manifestation if there is no basic resistance in the manifestation. So how can He destroy what we call devil? How can creation begin without intrinsic resistance? That’s why the law of resistance exists or Ramm. It is the principal that any manifestation involves resistance. “Fiat Lux,” to break the resistance of darkness, light was necessary. It is already there, basic, part of us, will be us. But this resistance you’ll find does not last, it is a period only. That’s why the scriptures say “all things comes to pass, but not to stay.” That was left out in the writings. All these things will come to pass, but not to say. Because all things are moving in the cosmological time sequence with their intrinsic resistance. Now, resistance acts only for a period until you recognize it as resistance and if you don’t recognize it as resistance, psychological, physical, or spiritual then it will continue to possess and haunt you, obsess you. But it can’t stay too long either because the very law of nature it is moving. It is not static. It is in the process of moving. 4 So we move from resistance to Adjustment or Adaptation, where we learn to adapt ourselves. So A stands for Adaptation. We are forced to adapt in spite of ourselves. Even adaptation can’t last too long, that changes too into Mutation, which really means change. So we say we live in a world of constant changes. When change has worked itself out, we have Mold or Pattern and it is set in its primary function as Life. The input of the function of Life is set. We have to have some output, which is Secondary Principle, then comes Saturation, we get bored. As we get bored of what we get molded into, it begins to drag upon us and that dragging is called a Lag or Boredom state. It is a non-incentive state. Right in this same lag, the period of non-incentive is coming into the period of incentive. Incentive exists in Lag because we get initiative coming out of it, we get a new impetus. Also called Night of the Soul, which leads to impetus, a spark, new incentive, new ID (idea). It is churning in our consciousness. And we move out with that new impetus to Recurrence, a new cycle. The cycle is based on a spiral movement, from the central / zero point of One. The darkness is the blackboard, moving out by intrinsic resistance gradually until it comes in line with the central point of One. The law of recurrence spirals out. Until Man knows he is Soul, he cannot free himself to have experience of his Being. You see the reason why the student has difficulty experiencing himself. This demonstrates the Christ conscious ability to materialize your thoughts at will. Peter realized that he had committed an act of pride. 1 He too (Peter) made the one mistake that Jesus was liable to make which is the last test of pride with the ego, you see. There is no devil and we say he went up to be tempted in the wilderness 40 days and 40 nights, fasting. He was hammering out the different aspects of ego and the various negative natures in it. The last one is, “If you bow down and worship me all these things are yours.” In other words, “I give you power over life and death if you only become a dictator over humanity.” The scripture say that man has the power to have dominion over the universe, but not to possess it. If the mind would stay in the present now, “Meekly wait and murmur not” in self-observation, then the mind would experience peace because the present is peace. It’s the gap between frustration and anxiety, between past and future, it is the eternal Now where you actually do live. It is the only reality. Now is the process of participation, you are in the presence all the time. In this nowness is expansion, it is an internal integration of the three forces in your mechanism: physical, mental, and spiritual. You are Soul and the connection between the Soul to a frame called the body lies in the breath: incoming and outgoing breath. This incoming / outgoing function is one of love, devotion, conscious recognition / identity / oneness. To stray from this point of reference from within one’s self is to go away from the source of peace and tranquility into the stream of agitation and tension. Now this word “I AM” does not refer to the body, now it refers to everything in this universe. So when you love your neighbor as yourself, that’s loving yourself as one another and isn’t that what Jesus used to say, “Love the Lord thy God with all your mind and heart and love your neighbor as yourself.” He was speaking mathematics too, but He didn’t come outright and hit you on the head and told you it was mathematics but you learn it today in school as mathematics, these two things are equal to the same thing and therefore they themselves are equal to each other. Easter Houston Part 1 - April 1969

Adano69_04_1EasterHoustonQ2RRNW6 - (Meditation). This is the resurrection of Jesus and it’s called “The first day of the week cometh and Mary Magdalene early, when it yet dark, unto the sepulchre, seeth the stone taken away from the sepulchre. Then she runneth, and cometh to Simon Peter, and to the other disciples, whom Jesus loved, and said unto them, They have taken away the Lord out of the sepulchre, and we know not where they have laid him.” And she said “Mary stood without at the sepulchre weeping: and as she wept, and stood down, and looked into the sepulchre, and seeth two angels in white sitting, one at the head, and the other end at the feet, where the body of Jesus had lain.” The Master Jesus did leave the frame and the angels are actually angelic beings in their astral bodies and “one and the head and one at the foot” is indication of adoration and devotion. See devotion is at the feet, adoration is at the head, “And they said unto her, Woman, why weepest thou? And she said unto them, because they have taken away my Lord,” that is devotion and adoration has withdrawn the Master Consciousness. “And I know not where thou hast laid. And when she said thus, she turned herself back, and saw Jesus standing, and knew not that it was Jesus.” In other words she was in the presence of the realized Master and His astral radial form, she did not recognize Him. “Jesus said unto her, Woman, why weepest thou? Whom seekest thou? And she supposing him to be the gardener, said unto him, Sir, if thou have borne him away hence tell me where thou hast laid him, and I will take him away. And Jesus saith unto her, Mary. She turned herself and said unto him, Rabboni,” which means Master or Guru, “which is to say, Master,” the Hebrew interpretation, Rabboni or Master or Guru means the same thing. In other words the disciple recognizes the Guru. “And Jesus said unto her, Touch me not,” well this is normal for the disciple when he sees his Guru to want to touch Him, even to touch His feet because this is where the vibrations come or touch His hand or any part of His body or prostrate himself and touch the Guru. That’s why He said “touch me not for I am not yet ascended to my Father: but go to my brethren, and say unto them, I ascend unto my Father, and your Father; and to my God, and your God.” Which is to say He’s still in a state of consciousness that is bordering between the vibratory and non-vibratory manifestation and the astral form is still pulsating with life. Now He did not want her to touch Him immediately because any negativeness on her part would have been transferred back to His body and kind of retard, it’s like trying to touch wet cement, it would leave an impression. He wanted to reach the stage where this mechanism was in a state of curing or completeness. So He says “I ascend unto My Father, your Father, My God, your God,” which is to say that the same principle, the same audible life stream that is passing through all of us draws us back up, we ascend through it. So go and tell His brethern, go and tell the disciples that He’s ascending, make them conscious that He is with them. “And Mary Magdalene came and told the disciples that she had seen the Lord, and that he had spoken these things unto her. Then the same day at evening, being the first day of the week, when the doors were shut where the disciples were assembled for the fear of the Jews, came Jesus and stood in the midst, and said unto them, Peace be unto you.” You see in that resurrected form, having no negativeness in it, it can pass through all material substances and make itself manifest. So He manifested Himself to His disciples in the room and because the room was locked up, there’s no way for Him to come through the door, but He was able to pass through the wall into the room by consciousness because He realized that matter was only consciousness and the He was pure consciousness now and therefore it was no boundary line or limitation to His consciousness where He can be and they were seeing for the first time in a new consciousness what the real consciousness of Jesus was in the room. They were seeing consciousness for the first time manifesting as energy and by saying “Peace be unto you,” that is to free them from agitation or fear or restlessness or their own personal guilts and hangups that they were suffering from and their own personal fear of being persecuted by the Jews or the Romans of the time and that they were in hiding at the same time so they had mental problems and they needed this peace to bring them back into harmony, into mental attunement with Himself. “And when he had so said, he shewed unto them his hands and his side. Then were the disciples glad, when they saw the Lord.” In other words, He had to give them tangible proof of His reality that He was not an apparition or a mental hallucination and this would allow them now to realize that He did transcend the limitation of matter by consciousness and He was a fully realized Master and the disciples were glad when they saw the Lord. “Then said Jesus to them again, Peace be unto you,” in other words it’s very important even at this stage although you’re seeing this mechanism, whatever doubts are still in your mind, you must still transmit this peace to free the mind so that the true Soul nature of the disciples can perceive now their Soul nature of the Master standing in front of them. “As my Father hath sent me, even so send I you,” in other words the audible life consciousness and the life power that’s manifesting in Jesus was not brought there by any ego, it was there to fulfill to the disciples that the Divinity was in Man and this is the same Divinity would have been projected back to them now as disciples to make them conscious of their own Divinity, that they too can achieve this realization. Fri 0:10 “So I send you,” that is to say “I now make it possible for you to realize where you are, make it possible for you to make the same effort to get there.” “And when he had said thus, he breathed on them,” this is very important, He breathed on them, that is He granted them another initiation, a new another level of awareness and at the same time He took away a great deal of karma from them because “God breathed into Man the breath of life and Man became a living Soul.” Now when a Master can breathe upon His disciples or project this, it’s another form of initiation, this Holy Breath, this Holy Consciousness can now free the disciples of many levels of karma and make the consciousness clearer. In other words it’s like blowing away the dust from a dirty object, the Master has blown away the psychological karma by His consciousness off his disciples by breathing on them. In other words He’s granted them another level of initiation. “And said unto them, Receive ye the Holy Ghost,” prepare now to absorb the audible life stream, He granted them initiation again, bringing them closer into the audible life stream or the Cosmic Sound or Holy Word or Holy Spirit. In other words the Holy Spirit is involved in sound, Its involved in breath, and when a Master transmits it, you are linked up to it and therefore your whole mechanism now is transformed but it took that much time preparation for them to get there, to get that particular gift. Sat They weren’t ready for it before and He had to eliminate it from them and this elimination or this bringing down of the Holy Spirit on these disciples of His was a way of showing His concern for them. It wasn’t for the people outside He did it, it was just these disciples because He knew these disciples had to go out and carry on this work, these disciples had to be able to lift up themselves to lift up others. So they themselves needed the first cleaning up, they needed the focusing of the Holy Spirit in them. It’s like a cup, you can’t pour anything into the cup until you clean it out if it’s dirty and since the consciousness of the disciples were clouded, He could not bring down the Holy Spirit into them and infuse them unless He cleared up their doubts and in breathing upon them, it symbolically of clearing up the mental doubts in their consciousness and transmitting this energy or cosmic vibration into their bodies so that they can now radiate it. “And he said unto them when he had breathed the breath on them, Receive ye the Holy Ghost,” accept this energy, this is your definite life. “Whose soever sins ye remit,” now you got the power, whoever karma you remit, whoever sins you remit, whichever person’s karma you meet now “they are remitted unto them,” they’re cancelled out. Sun So you see Jesus didn’t come to save the sins of the world because He’s passed on now and He had to transfer His knowledge, He had to transfer the Holy Contact, who is He going to transfer it to but His disciples to whom which He was training and by giving them the same authority, the same power of consciousness now like Him, He was giving them ability to carry on the work. So He said, “whose soever sins ye remit,” whose soever karma you come in contact or cancel out or take on, the Guru takes on the karma of the disciples, this is called sin, these sins, these karma are remitted unto them, it’s cancelled out. “And whose soever sins ye retain, they are retained,” that is to say which karma is not being paid off or held in check until time is due, that particular karma for that individual is held. Some people come, they are very egotistical and would like to be forced to have their karma removed or like to see demonstrations of removal of karma, these type of people He’s telling His disciples in a way are retained, held back, don’t do nothing, stop, cut open their ego and hold them in check, let them learn their lesson. End “But Thomas, one of the twelve, called Didymus, was not with them when Jesus came. The other disciples therefore said unto him, We have seen the Lord. But he said unto them, Except I shall see in his hands the print of the nails, and put my finger into the print of the nails, and thrust my hand into his side, I will not believe.” Well this has two meanings, one meaning is that we may say that Thomas was a cynic and outright in disbelieving or doubting and this would be the layman’s interpretation of Thomas and this would be a classification you would give to Thomas that he was a doubting individual, very skeptical in every form, cynical type of individual, but in the higher truth it was not so. Thomas was a very scientific minded individual and knew the difference between hallucination, mesmerism, hypnotism, operation because it was very prevalent at the time as ESP is very prevalent today and many of the Jews in those days dabbled in it so they were well versed in it to the extent that Thomas wanted now the real truth, a real mystical fact, a real transcendence of consciousness over matter, not just consciousness over another person’s consciousness or the mere figment of imagination to say “well I saw such-and-such a person,” but you have no way to prove it. Thomas wanted something from a scientific aspect, he wanted the reality, so from his realization and knowing the structure of matter and its qualities and knowing from his study of meditation with the Master Jesus, he wanted to be positive that this was not just another figment of imagination that if resurrection was a reality or it was just another mental concept. Therefore he says “I will not believe until I have the proof” and after eight days again, you see how long it took? Eight days His disciples were with Him, that same building, Thomas was with them, then came Jesus. Now eight days after resurrection, eight days after crucifixion, where is the body of Jesus, where is it walking, where is it eating, where is it living, is it an apparition? An apparition may only, or a haunted place may only, have occasionally something happen at night and somebody say that saw some kind of a gossamer looking thing, but here is something it’s not happening at night, it is happening in broad daylight and it’s got to be a whole lot difference. “And Thomas with them: then came Jesus, the doors being shut, and stood in the midst, and said, Peace be unto you.” His greeting again is significant at the period and at the time of the day and in the same building. Now if you say the building is haunted then what time of the day was it being haunted, you see, and if it’s haunted would the message be the same thing, “Peace be unto you,” “why the hell don’t you get out of this place.” This would be the normal way a ghost would come to anybody to scare the living daylights out of them, he wouldn’t want you to have any sense of reality or peace. So the experience is of a high spiritual nature. “Then said Jesus to Thomas, Reach hither thy finger, and behold my hands; and reach hither thy hand, and thrust it into my side: and be not faithless, but believing. “There’s a big difference in that statement knowing now that it was not doubting Thomas, “be not faithless.” 0:20 Man’s faith is often shaken by doubt but that does not make a man faithless. A man is only faithless if there is no evidence as to the reality of his spiritual development, then there is a condemnation as to what efforts he’s doing, so there’s a big difference between a man is faithless and a man is doubtful. You can have doubt and you still may question, but to be faithless is to say that there is absolutely no way to prove anything, you see, and if there is a way to prove something then faith is always there, faith is something has a chance to grow now, it grows from the evidence of things not only seen or believed but evidence from the things that are inherent in the person’s consciousness that he intuitively feel is there and now has a chance to express itself, this restores faith. If it can’t by any form of intuition manifest itself then it will become faithless, there would be no faith, without intuition you could not establish this faith. So Jesus is saying to Thomas not to be faithless is not to let his intuition fail him and what he intuitively feel about what is happening in front of him is genuine so learn to rely on your intuition and not on your intellect or reason and believe, “be not faithless but believing.” Now believing is not necessarily the mere fact that you accept something without question because true belief is to know and true belief is not superstition. So Thomas was experiencing true belief by trying to know for the first time what actually took place in the life of Jesus, whereas the others might believe but not fully comprehend but because they want to be not left out in the crowd, they would not appear to question the Master. Now when you never question the Master as to what is happening, you never really know for sure what you are receiving is genuine. You may only go so far in your comprehension and this is what you would accept as happening as truth from a Master, but if you do question without any form of ego in a true sincere questioning, then real faith, real understanding begins to manifest. That’s why we question not for the sake of tearing down the Master or for the sake of trying to prove that we know something or we have any better answer, we only question in relation to get a better understanding of what we are experiencing in order to direct ourselves actively when we are using it. “And Thomas answered and said unto him, My Lord and my God.” First “my Lord” is indicative that this is the true Guru, this is the Master, this is the one who has demonstrated through physical power by living in the physical body and transcending death, but he who can transcend death in a physical body must be God. Two things are equal to the same thing are themselves equal to one another. So the Lord and God, the Guru and God is one and the same thing made manifest in the human body through the experience of discipleship we see the reality of it by being exposed to it, otherwise there is no relationship between the disciple and the Guru let alone to accept the Guru as a living proof of God. So our first realization is “He is Lord,” Lord of himself, Radha Soami, Lord of the Soul, and then on top of the bargain, He is God manifest the whole creative process because wherever it is going to be possible for the Creator to manifest, it would be to the extent He is Master over death because God is total life, total audible life and there is no death in life. So the Guru is a living example of God in life in form or matter, bringing the disciple back by the same process. So the Guru must bestow on the disciple that inherent knowledge, that inherent power, equal unto Himself. He could not make that disciple less than Himself, He has to give him exactly the same thing. “And Jesus said unto him, Thomas, because thou hast seen me, thou hast believed: blessed are they that have not seen, and yet have believed.” This is a way of admonishing the disciple that both aspects of realization are valid. We must question, we must have evidence, but we must not be gullible just to believe and not question and to say it is blessed to have believed and not seen, that is to say if the intuition is capable of transcending reason, that you can perceive within yourself and know that this reality is possible and that this reality has occurred, this inner realization is blessedness. To see the Guru outside of you is one, to see the Guru inside of you is greater because your whole meditation primarily as you advance in the years is to see Guru inside of you, to see God inside of you. Not so much to see God as the human form outside which has made it possible for you to recognize or grant you the initiation or grant you the instruction how to look inside because that’s what initiation is to show you how to look inside and what to look for. The great realization is after you have done that and then begin to see the Guru inside and the Guru is always present there when you go inside and make the effort to go up into yourself, make an effort to separate yourself from this physical body, He will always meet you there and take you on further inside of yourself, this is the blessedness, this is more important, you see, but this is not going inside by sheer belief and blind faith, this is going inside with the knowledge that this is the way back to God, that’s a big difference than thinking is supposed to be the way back. There’s a big difference between supposing it’s the way back inside by looking inside than realizing this is the only true way back because there’s no other way outside to bring you back, you see, and this is to make you realize that what you see outside is not everything, though it is tangible evidence to a certain extent but it’s limited evidence, it is going inside where the true belief begins, where the true knowledge begins, the true evidence of understanding begins, this is infinite, this is unlimited, this is blessedness, this is grace, this is freedom that you can know, shut your consciousness, and transport yourself in. “And many other signs truly did Jesus in the presence of his disciples, which are not written in this book.” Now it shows that a Master, even after having done certain things to satisfy the disciple, still keep on doing many more tangible things to satisfy the disciple because it’s not so easy for the disciple’s mind to grasp the significance of permanency of life after death. No one can tell you what exists after death if you never come back to tell you and whatever anyone would come back to tell you after death may still be a hallucination as far as you are concerned, you have no way to prove it because you never walk out beyond the door to see what is over on the other side of the scale and you have a living example telling you words are not sufficient, evidence of the body is not sufficient. 0:30 There must be more tangible signs in order to impregnate and impress this consciousness that is so saturated with the limitation of the world around it in order to free it from those limitations to comprehend the reality, the eternalness of the spirit beyond the grave, this requires more signs or more demonstrations of that spiritual nature. So if the books cannot record these signs and what makes reference to it, it stands to reason that many of these signs we may not even begin to comprehend or have no true inner knowledge of comprehending it unless we are going to experience it ourselves. There would be no sense of writing down these experience for people who have no understanding of it, let alone not having an opportunity to experience it but yet nevertheless to make reference that it was there and it did happen, you see. “But these are written,” those signs, those conditions that were experienced were written down, “that you might believe that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of God; and that believing ye might have life through his name.” Now this statement is very particular “but these were written that you might believe that Jesus is the Christ, the Son of God.” Now they did not say that you might believe that Jesus Christ is the only Son of God, big difference, it is written that you might believe or it is written so that you may understand the structure of creation that the man Jesus is the Christ, that the man Jesus achieved the Christ Consciousness and that the Christ Consciousness IS the Son of the Creative Consciousness and that every man who attains Christ Consciousness has retained or identified his true Son-ship with God. So every Master IS Christ manifesting back, not Jesus, every Master is the Christ, is that Son-ship, is that particular level of development that is inherent in the God Consciousness that Man will see all the time. “And that believing ye might have life through his name,” have life through His name. When you believe that the living manifestation of a Guru is the Christ Principle which is the eternal audible life principle of God and the two things being the same thing, one is vibratory and one is non-vibratory and if you are fortunate to be initiated and drawn into it, you will have the same experience of eternal life. Believing in that name, not the name Jesus now, believing in that cosmic audible life stream, the Naam, the cosmic power that is passing through that Guru sitting in front of you, that same force that is coming down from the Cosmic Intelligence, God, and flowing through the body as the Christ Intelligence that is being transmitted to you as initiation, this principle, this link is eternal life all the time, manifesting all the time. So every time a Master lives on the earth plane, He is manifesting this three-fold principle: God, the eternal life, Christ principle in the body form as Master-hood, and the transference to the disciple in initiation as the Holy Spirit, a link from there to here to there all the time. So “none cometh unto the Father but by Me, “ you got to pass through this mechanism, you gotta pass through this link, you see, and in His name, not Jesus name, in the name of the Christ Principle present in every living Master, does the disciple return back to the Creative Intelligence through that link-up, through that name, through that cosmic sound, through that cosmic meditational contact of initiation are we drawn back through this filter, which you call the Christ Principle in man, back into the pure Cosmic Consciousness. Now here is an object, we have right inside here the film which we can call the Creative Intelligence and we have a filter here to hold the light in and we have an object through which we photograph. Now this lens here passes the light, you press the switch, the picture is recorded, but if it doesn’t pass through that lens, it cannot record on the film and this is exactly the same thing, “no man come unto the Father,” light of the image cannot be recorded on the film by exposing a film in front of it “except by Me,” except it passes through a filter, except it passes through a lens and a lens has to do with concentration, focusing. So no man’s consciousness, no man’s liberation, can come to him except he passes through a Guru, or a Guru’s consciousness, or a Christ consciousness present in a Guru who is the living Lord and who is God at the same time manifesting as form. So it is this that Jesus is emphasizing, when the disciple wrote it, “but these were written,” these particular incidents were written “that you might believe,” that you may understand now that Jesus at that period is the Christ, has the Christ Consciousness present within Himself, the Sun of God, not the only Sun of God, the Sun of God, that this Christ Principle is the radiant light of God Consciousness, that all individuals who enter the Christ Consciousness they become Suns of God. Now Jesus Himself would say, “know ye not that ye are gods?” “And as many as received Him, to them gave He the power to become Suns of God.” Now “as many as received Him” and He says “received the Holy Spirit” when He came to them and He blew upon them and let them receive the Holy Spirit. They say unto him, We also go with thee. They went forth, and entered into a ship immediately; and that night they caught nothing.” “And that night they caught nothing,” they all went fishing but they caught nothing. “But when the morning was now come and Jesus stood on the shore: but the disciples knew not that it was Jesus.” You see even after He’s manifesting Himself so many times to them after death, their minds were still clouded because the radiance of His countenance blocks out any identification of Him and He’s standing there on the shore and they cannot recognize Him because His countenance is too bright. Their own limited mind cannot perceive outlines now, but then His voice, “Then Jesus saith unto them, Children, have ye any meat? And they answered him, No. And he said unto them, Cast the net on the right side of the ship, and ye shall find. They cast therefore, and now they were not able to draw it for the multitude of fishes.” And then they realized their Guru was still with them, even in the smallest details of sustenance, even after death. So the Guru don’t forsake you when He’s gone out of the body, He’s always with you. 0:40 “Therefore that disciple whom Jesus loved saith unto Peter, It is the Lord. Now when Simon Peter heard that it was the Lord, he girt his fisher’s coat unto him, (for he was naked,) and did cast himself into the sea.” Well here is the boat and there is the seashore and there is the Guru standing there and if you have any love for the Guru, the first thing you want to do is run up and greet your Guru because everybody is… see in India in all the pictures everybody trying to run and grab ahold of the Guru’s feet, so the love of Simon Peter when he heard that this was his Master standing on the seashore, he didn’t care how far the water is from the boat to the seashore, he just put on his coat and jumped in the water to go and meet the Guru, this is the love he has, and the other disciples came in with the ship, they rowed the ship in, “(for they were not far from land, but as it were two hundred cubits,) dragging the net with fishes. As soon then as they were come to land, they saw a fire of coals there, and fish laid thereon, and bread.” Now they didn’t make the fire, they didn’t make the bread, and if the manifestation of Jesus after death was an apparition, bread and fire can’t put itself together by no amount of apparitions, there ain’t no ghost in this world that can put it together, you understand. So He has to be a realized Master, He has to have a form that is radiant, but it casts no shadow and leaves no footprint, but it’s solid flesh and blood all the same and it can eat like you and I, this is liberation. And they said they saw fish laid on the fire and bread and “Jesus said unto them, Bring of the fish which ye have now caught. Simon Peter went up, and drew the net to land full of great fishes, an hundred and fifty and three: and for all there were too many, yet was not the net broken. Jesus said unto them, Come and dine. And none of the disciples durst ask him, Where art thou? knowing that it was the Lord.” Intuition now for the first time made them recognize that this was truly a Master, it is truly their own Master, no more questioning “who are you, where were you, what were you doing?” You see all that is gone now, consciousness is clean, they’re for the first time in the presence of this love, this love is so great and “Jesus then cometh, and taketh bread, and giveth them, and fish likewise. This is now the third time that Jesus shewed himself to his disciples, after that he was risen from the dead.” See He gave them many actual experiences, first He manifested and He spoke, second time He let them touch Him, the third time He’s feeding them He’s going to eat with them. Now a Master has said anytime a spiritual experience occurs and you see one of these Masters manifesting to you, these are the three tests you make. One, let Him talk to you and let Him show you His feet that you can see both feet together at the same time that you can reach out and touch. Second, He should be able to come up and embrace you. And third, you should be able to offer Him food that He would eat part of it and leave the other part and it don’t rot after He’s gone. Then you know you’ve had a genuine experience with a Master, no matter what level you are, that this is your devotion and when you meditate, you meditate on all the Masters and which One wants to grant you His darshan, He alone comes and grants it. That doesn’t say He has to be in the body or out of the body, this is the way they grant you darshan, this is the way they grant you their spiritual blessing, but your living Master will help you to get there too. He’s there to open the doors, but these are the three things that are evidence of how to test these people or these real Masters when you get the experience. So Yogananda used to say, “you can see all the Masters present, all who’ve passed on, if you have the devotion and these are the ways you test them.” Once a person says he’s seen a Master, you ask him how many times he’s seen this Master and what are the three things he’s put the Master to the test or if he’s just having a mental hallucination. You see the scriptures made sure, Thomas was a scientist, he made sure that these things were recorded, that we weren’t being fooled. He wanted not only what he saw, he wanted to be able to feel, he wanted to be certain that that thing could eat like him and all three are here, all three tests. They first saw Jesus in the house, the second time they were given an opportunity to feel the body, the third time He’s feeding them, feeding them solid substances. “So when they had dined, Jesus said to Simon Peter, Simon, son of Jonas, lovest thou me more than these?” Now here’s the test, after you have all these evidence that this is a Guru, that this is a real genuine Master, then He’s going to ask you the one big thing, “Do you love Me more than these miracles, do you love Me really as the living reality God, more than all these type of inner experiences, which you prefer?” Now He’s putting the disciple to the test. He gave the disciple the three proof that He was a Master, now He wants to see what love does the disciple want now, which is more important, these miracles, these particular inner experiences, these spiritual experiences, are they more important than the love for God? You see this is the test, that’s why he says “so when they have dined,” He satisfied all their intellectual and physical problem now, He test them now their spiritual problems. “Jesus said to Simon Peter, Simon, son of Jonas, lovest thou me more than these? He said unto him, Yea, Lord; thou knowest that I love thee. and he said unto him again,” Jesus said to him “ok if you love Me, Feed my lambs.” If you really love Me and you don’t care for these miracles, then render service to those around you, they’re like lambs, they are searching for the truth, they are reaching out. Because a lamb is not easily excited, a lamb don’t want no miracle to tell him that the shephard is nearby, you see. So “if you love Me,” if you truly love Me and you have no concern for miraculous things, you would be willing to render humble service now to all those who come to you for spiritual upliftment without utilizing miraculous things to make them understand themselves. So this is what He’s trying to tell Peter now, “wake up,” if you really want to understand unconditional love, you really want to do something now, “feel my lambs” means render service, take care of these devotees, and see that they understand the truth about themselves without resorting to miraculous principles. And “He said to him again the second time,” first He’s testing him physically of his love, now He’s testing him again the second time mentally of his love, “Simon, son of Jonas, lovest thou me? He said unto him, Yea, Lord; thou knowest that I love thee.” First it’s physical, “I love you Lord! Why are you getting over aggravated, I love You,” it’s the psychological part. And He says, “Feed my sheep.” The lambs was first and second was sheep, physical things are childlike, people who start out in search of truth are like lambs, they don’t know, they don’t question, there’s no argument. 0:50 Intellectual people question therefore the second level is in the mind now, “if you love me feed my sheep.” I want to know now deep down in your own mental makeup now if you really love Me and you don’t have no reservation to mentally question then you can cope with those people who will question you as to what you’re teaching. So take care and look after the people who come to you, like sheep now they’re gonna “baaaah,” they’re gonna try and bark you down or bray you down until you prove things to them. “And he said unto him the third time, Simon, son of Jonas, lovest thou me?” He’s testing him now spiritually. “Peter was grieved,” first it was a physical test, “Yeah I love you Lord, why should I not?” The second time “but Lord I love You,” you’re reaching now to the psychological nature, but you don’t get grieved. He says the third time Peter was grieved, you are hitting the whole spiritual structure of the man now. “Am I really warranting the love of my Master? Is my Master really testing me or something? Now I’m getting at the very core of myself. Am I losing His love for me, am I going to lose His grace?” This is really getting you in turmoil now. What is he going through after all this, what am I going through now? So “Peter was grieved because he said unto him the third time, Lovest thou me? And he said unto him, Lord, thou knowest all things,” Guru you know, you know if I love you or not, you know mentally, physically, and spiritually if I love, why are you asking? It’s like Ananda Moyi, who met Yogananda, Yogananda asked him three times if there were fishes sick people in Switzerland or not and he says “yes there were” and the fourth day when he go to ask him the same question before he could ask him the question, “Yes there are sick people fishes in Switzerland.” He started to say it like a parrot, you see, it’s the same here. “All things thou knowest that I love thee. And Jesus said unto him, Feed my sheep.” Now the second time sheep, the third time sheep, and the first time lambs. There’s a big difference, a lamb don’t question, it accepts full surrender, a sheep questions and the full grown sheep is mature and can handle itself but it need guidance. A spiritual person after he has come home to a certain understanding, he’s mature, all he needs is a certain guidance and he’s free. He said “Feed my sheep. Verily, verily, I say unto thee, When thou wast young, thou girdedst thyself, and walkedst whither thou wouldest,” just like the sheep, “but when thou shalt be old, thou shalt stretch forth thy hands, and another shall gird thee, and carry thee whither thou wouldest not.” That’s the sheep now. See when you are young, the lambs walk where they want and you have enough gumption and ego you get up and walk where you want and when you are old, like a full grown sheep, you need a sheepdog to guide you where you’re supposed to go, you need someone to gird you or guide you along, you need direction more so than when you were young, follow me? Because you’re liable to make more mistakes when you’re advanced because every mistake can be detrimental because you know, whereas when you’re young you don’t know and therefore you’re forgiven. When you’re mature you’re supposed to know and supposed to be able to discriminate and select so you don’t make mistakes so you need guidance. “This spake he, signifying by what death he should glorify God. And when he had spoken this, he saith unto him, Follow me. Then Peter, turning about, seeth the disciple whom Jesus loved following; which also leaned on his breast at supper, and said, Lord, which is he that betrayeth thee?” See Jesus was speaking to Peter and behind Peter was John and “Peter seeing him said to Jesus, Lord, and what shall this man do?” Well Jesus was giving counsel to Peter by saying “if you love Me, after you’ve had all these experiences, if you love Me, do the work, go out and teach.” Now Peter realized that he had tremendous devotion but also realized that this other man had an inner communion with, or inner link with the Master, this man would have no outward work to do, but this is not really true, this is Peter’s way of thinking. Hear how the Guru answers him, “And Jesus said unto him, If I will that he tarry till I come, what is that to thee? follow me.” Now this is very very mystical statement, very very mystical, it’s not a literal statement because it was taken literally by Peter. This is Peter’s literal understanding of that statement, “Then went this saying abroad among the brethren, that that disciple should not die.” You see this was the literal understanding of the statement when He said “if I will that he tarry till I come, what is that to thee? follow me.” Now before He made this statement and before Peter made any request, Jesus was describing to him that he’s young he had his own way and when he’s old he has to guided and Peter literally took that as the way he was gonna die. So if that’s the way he’s gonna die, then he says “this is to surely glorify God and when he had spoken he said unto him, follow me, and Peter thought this is the way he’s supposed to die.” So when he gets old somebody take care of him, not realizing that this has to do with spiritual principles. So he automatically, realizing that “well here is my way of going out of this body, but what about this other guy, how is he going to go out of his body, what’s he got? So when he asks he gets an answer and he jumps to the wrong conclusion, the wrong conclusion is that “went this saying went abroad among the brethren, that that disciple should not die: yet Jesus said not unto him,” Jesus didn’t say that unto the man, that he would not die, “He shall not die; yet Jesus said not unto him, He shall not die,” Jesus did not say that to the man, Jesus said “If I will that he tarry till I come, what is that to thee? Follow me.” And this statement was assumed by the brethren that this man would never die, yet Jesus, it is pointed out here again in the next paragraph, Jesus never said that unto the man that he would not die. So it goes to show you that they do not understand this statement. If He never said that the man would not die, “but, If I will that he tarry till I come, what is that to thee?” This is a big difference, what does this statement really mean? This is the disciple which testify now, this disciple who is testifying, who is writing this thing, this disciple is the guy who everybody thought is not gonna die and this is the disciple who Jesus says “if I will that he tarry till I come, what is that to thee,” this is the man who is writing. “This is the disciple which testifieth of these things, and wrote these things: and we know that his testimony is true. And there are also many other things which Jesus did, the which, if they should be written every one, I suppose that even the world itself could not contain the books that should be written.” But you see, the disciple to whom this statement was made, “if I will that he tarry till I come, what is that to thee, follow me,” this has a tremendous deep spiritual meaning. 1:00 It had nothing to do with physical body, is had to do with spiritual relationship. Jesus was the embodiment of pure intuition, the intuitive Christ principle in the body, and Peter was the embodiment of willpower in the human body, the driving force which is necessary to mold anything on this earth. Now John is Bhatki or love, devotion, and Jesus is saying “if I will that he tarry,” if I make it possible that his willpower stays in that state of attunement, that is to tarry, “until I come,” until intuition descends upon him, “what is that to you,” whose an embodiment of willpower right now. You, Peter, is an embodiment of willpower, not an embodiment of devotion and intuition, he’s an embodiment of devotion because you are pointing out how devotion this man is to Me, you’re the guy who’s pointing out what is gonna happen to this guy and I’m saying, I am the intuition, I am the Divine intuitive nature and you are willpower, but you are not intuition, you’re not in that intuitive state and though he explains certain little things, where Peter traveled and where Peter went, but it does not explain the intricacies of the spiritual life because it did not have the devotion, it did not have the intuition, Peter was strictly willpower. Now Jesus is trying to point out to the will or in a higher understanding, intuition is saying to willpower, “suspend yourself until intuition comes into you, then you will have both intuition and will and devotion,” and every man must pass through this particular type of growth, he must have intuition, will, and devotion and if Peter was going to die the way he literally took it, that someone is going to lead him by the hand until he dies, we found out he didn’t die that way either. He decided to be crucified upside down. Now why did he decide to be crucified upside down, the realization came to him after what the meaning meant, that it didn’t mean that John the disciple would tarry until Jesus comes 1000 years from now and never die, it dawned on him that it didn’t mean that no more because he started to picture the thing, he realized that he was an embodiment of will and will is an obstacle in the path of intuition and will must succumb to intuition, it must surrender to intuition so by choosing death upside down was symbolical of saying, “I the will now has surrendered to intuition, the Lord in Man,” and this was his way of symbolically dying, physically doing it to say “well I realize now what is the truth, I am free,” and in that way he chose an upside down death symbolically of his freedom and, in a literal sense, for those who did’t understand because if you didn’t understand in a literal sense, “oh because he denied the Lord and the Lord died the other way, so he’s gonna die this way just to be different, to show his respect to the Lord.” He died upside down primarily to show, as an embodiment of will, it had to surrender to intuition which is Christ principle and that John, who was an embodiment of devotion, had to remain with that devotion and will in a state of attunement or tarrying until intuition descended into him and when it descended into him, then was he able to be a testimony or a witness of the things that occurred and record them. So John was then definitely the disciple to which all the inner mysteries of the Christ life became known because it will take intuition to convey to intuition the innermost secrets of the Christ consciousness, it could not take intuition to convey to the will what occurs because the will could never recognize intuition. A man’s intuition is not recognizable by his will, it takes his intuition to recognize the higher intuition in himself, that there is a link. So when we look into God, we look into God not by will, but by intuition and devotion, then coupled by the will through persistency to stick with it. So we have all three flowing as one. So we see in the disciple John, a manifestation of all the forces for the first time and therefore Jesus was able to transmit to that disciple what He wanted to transmit. Thank you.
